#  file: fsfDeveloperProjects2010-May.txt
#  package: fsfRawData
#  description of file/package:
#
#  This package includes raw data files from our database of Free Software 
#  Foundation project information generated from the list of projects gathered 
#  in 2010-May
#
#  Scripts & raw data available at http://flossmole.org
#  Scripts written by Megan Squire and contributed to the FLOSSmole project
#
#  This data is free and available for any use (after all we just spidered it ;)
#  We do however request that those using the data in any published form provide 
#  a citation to: FLOSSmole Project (2004-2010) 
#  The project is available at: http://flossmole.org
#  
#  SELECT dp.person_name, dp.proj_num, p.proj_unixname, dp.role, dp.email, dp.web_page, dp.date_collected, dp.datasource_id 
#  FROM fsf_developer_projects dp, fsf_projects p 
#  WHERE dp.proj_num = p.proj_num AND dp.datasource_id=221 
#  ORDER BY p.proj_unixname, dp.person_name
#
#  datasource_id = 221 is the 2010-May collection from FSF.
